declare @ctrlStates int
begin
select @ctrlStates=CtrlStates from [IceHockeySchedules] with(nolock) where webid='McV9Ouwc'
IF @ctrlStates=0 OR @ctrlStates=2
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = '0',[RB] = '0',[TrackerText] ='',[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1,[StatusText]='19' where webid='McV9Ouwc' AND GameType='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=1
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[TrackerText] ='',[StatusText] = '19',[Record]=NULL,[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '19',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
end

end

begin

end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '18',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end

begin

begin

end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=1
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[TrackerText] ='',[StatusText] = '17',[Record]=NULL,[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '17',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
end

declare @ctrlStates int
begin
select @ctrlStates=CtrlStates from [IceHockeySchedules] with(nolock) where webid='McV9Ouwc'
IF @ctrlStates=0 OR @ctrlStates=2
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = '0',[RB] = '0',[TrackerText] ='',[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1,[StatusText]='16' where webid='McV9Ouwc' AND GameType='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=1
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[TrackerText] ='',[StatusText] = '16',[Record]=NULL,[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '16',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
end

end

begin

end

begin

begin

begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = '0',[RB] = '0',[TrackerText] ='',[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1,[StatusText]='12' where webid='McV9Ouwc' AND GameType='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=1
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[TrackerText] ='',[StatusText] = '12',[Record]=NULL,[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '12',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
end

declare @ctrlStates int
begin
select @ctrlStates=CtrlStates from [IceHockeySchedules] with(nolock) where webid='McV9Ouwc'
IF @ctrlStates=0 OR @ctrlStates=2
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = '0',[RB] = '0',[TrackerText] ='',[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1,[StatusText]='11' where webid='McV9Ouwc' AND GameType='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=1
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[TrackerText] ='',[StatusText] = '11',[Record]=NULL,[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '11',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
end

end

begin

end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '10',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'

declare @ctrlStates int
begin
select @ctrlStates=CtrlStates from [IceHockeySchedules] with(nolock) where webid='McV9Ouwc'
IF @ctrlStates=0 OR @ctrlStates=2
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = '0',[RB] = '0',[TrackerText] ='',[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1,[StatusText]='9' where webid='McV9Ouwc' AND GameType='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=1
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [GameStates] ='S',[TrackerText] ='',[StatusText] = '9',[Record]=NULL,[GameDate]='2015-08-14',[GameTime]='13:00',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
ELSE IF @ctrlStates=3
begin
UPDATE [IceHockeySchedules] SET [RunsA] ='0,0',[RunsB] = '0,0',[RA] = 0,[RB] = 0,[StatusText] = '9',[ChangeCount] =[ChangeCount]+1 where webid='McV9Ouwc' and gametype='IHBF'
end
end
